byte-identical for extras-free callers (/api/ask, MCP recall тАФ tests unmodified, deep-equal proof); second drive-by fix: refusal citation-strip was gated on note-style `citedSourcesIn` so an extra-category citation could survive on a refusal тАФ now unconditional. тЬУ RETROFIT SHIPPED (2026-07-10, same day): plain `muse ask` now routes through `streamGroundedRecall` тАФ seam grew `composeSystemPrompt` / `normalizeAnswer` (pre-gate, buffered-only) / `extraChunks` / `result.scored` + `preRefusalStrippedCitations`, all byte-identical-when-absent; persona rides the runtime adapter (`composeChatSystemContent`); verdict layer + presentation stay CLI-side over the seam result; cli 3384 green unmodified, eval:self-improving 35/35, smoke:live 23/23. тЧж REMAINING follow-ups: (a) `--with-tools` still runs legacy assembly тАФ needs a prepare-only seam entry point (context+gate without the seam driving generation); (b) live-delta fence-marker strip (`stripGroundingFences`) applies to the final answer only, not per-delta (rare defensive backstop, deferred); (c) `/api/ask` responses now carry `result.scored` (full prompt-window chunks) тАФ consider an API-side trim if payload size matters; - тЬУ GROUNDING EDGE fix (found by probing the real ask path тАФ grounding-side dogfood): the citation-RECALL check (`reportCitationRecall`) falsely flagged an honest ABSTENTION ("I'm afraid I do not have a specific timeтАж") as "matches your notes but carries no citation". Root cause: a broad evidence union (the note + 20 tasks + 4 reminders) inflated token overlap so the abstention looked 'citable', then was flagged as uncited тАФ PUNISHING the exact behavior the edge wants (abstain over fabricate). Fix: `isAbstentionSentence` (EN+KO self-knowledge negation) excludes abstentions from the citable set. agent-core 2692 + citation-recall-abstention 13 (incl. a REGRESSION GUARD that a genuine uncited claim is still flagged) + mutation (drop the guard тЖТ RED) + LIVE re-probe (same question, the false тЪая╕П warning is gone, abstention + `[from тАж]` citation intact). The edge's fabrication=0 held throughout both probes (no fabricated time); this hardens its PRECISION (no false warning on honesty).
- тЬУ OPS BOARD dogfooding (Jinan-picked: validate real usage, not just mechanism). Driving a real addтЖТexpandтЖТrunтЖТshow lifecycle surfaced + fixed 3 friction gaps a user hits immediately: (1) `board show <id>` тАФ a done container's synthesized answer was stored but unreadable from the CLI except `--json` (now shows status/deps/runs/result via formatTaskDetail); (2) `board rm <id>` тАФ could add but never delete (removeTask, prunes dangling deps); (3) `board run` progress feedback тАФ a slow local-model run printed nothing until a task FINISHED (looked hung); now `тЦ╕ running: <task>тАж` before each agent call. All live-verified. LESSON: mechanism-complete тЙа usable тАФ the CRUD/feedback gaps only showed by actually USING it. Minor follow-up left: `board clear` (rm covers it). Next direction options unchanged: cloud live round-trip (needs user key) ┬╖ return to the grounding/learning CORE edge (untouched this session тАФ the actual moat).
- тЬУ OPS BOARD zombie/liveness recovery (the last assessment gap vs hermes). `staleInProgressTasks`/`reclaimStaleTasks` (pure): a task stuck `in_progress` past a window (30 min default, `MUSE_BOARD_STALE_MS`) = a crashed run (the board is otherwise synchronous) тЖТ moved to `blocked`, NOT auto-re-queued (a crash may have half-applied a side effect + the in-memory dedup is gone, so auto-rerun = double-execute тАФ outbound-safety, same hazard as resume). `muse board reclaim` + auto-reclaim at the top of `board run` (a zombie would else block its dependents forever). multi-agent 327 + cli board 23 + mutation (reclaimтЖТtodo тЖТ the no-auto-requeue test RED) + live (`board reclaim` unstuck a zombie тЖТ blocked+reason). тЬУ visual UI DONE тАФ `GET /api/board` (board-routes.ts, read-only feed of the same persisted board the CLI drives, injectable listTasks) + a web Kanban `BoardView` (columns todoтЖТdone, container/synthesis badges, dep counts, blockedReason, horizontal-scroll bounded inside `.content`) wired into NAV (key "b") + i18n. api board-routes 2/2 + real-browser verify (Playwright: heading "ы│┤ыУЬ", columns render, container/review/blocked cards shown, `.content` 968px bounded in a 1200px viewport тАФ no blowout). OPS BOARD now feature-complete incl. the UI; only WRITE actions from the web (add/move/run) remain optional.

- тЬУ OPS MULTI-AGENT тАФ durable Kanban board, S1тАУS6 COMPLETE (2026-06-28, Jinan pivot to match openclaw/hermes). `@muse/multi-agent`: **S1** pure board core (`task-board.ts` тАФ dependency-gated `nextReadyTask`, transitions, retry-with-reason) ┬╖ **S2** `board-store.ts` FileAgentTaskBoard (atomic persist, missing/corruptтЖТ[]) ┬╖ **S3** `dispatch-board.ts` `dispatchNextTask` (next-ready тЖТ injected executor тЖТ outcome folded back; thrownтЖТblocked; retry replays prior reason) ┬╖ **S5** `tasksFromSubtasks` (decompositionтЖТboard tasks, dependsOn = fan-in gate) ┬╖ **S6** `resolveReview` + executor `needsReview` (outbound parks in REVIEW, approveтЖТdone/rejectтЖТblocked). **S4** `muse board` CLI (add/list/move/retry/review/run; outbound titles drafted+parked, never sent тАФ executor has NO transmission path at all). Verified: multi-agent 310 + cli board 12 + mutation + live (standalone `board run` completed a real agent task; store+dispatch+review live round-trip; retry-with-reason live) + independent evaluator PASS (outbound-safety deterministic). тЬУ FOLLOW-UP #1: the `board run` executor now runs each task through the real `agentRuntime.run` (tools + grounding + the agent loop), NOT a single generate тАФ proven live (a task used `muse.math.evaluate` + completed); a fail-closed `boardToolApprovalGate` allows READ tools but DENIES write/execute (an unattended run never auto-sends тАФ outbound stays the review column's job), and a retry replays the prior failure into the prompt. cli board 15 + mutation + test:changed 1334. тЬУ FOLLOW-UP #2 BOARD-AS-HANDOFF: a complex task EXPANDS into a sub-task DAG. `expandTaskIntoSubtasks` (pure) spawns the sub-tasks as a sequential chain (s_i deps s_{i-1}, matching decomposeRequest's ordered steps), rewires the parent to depend on them all + flags it `decomposed` тЖТ it becomes a CONTAINER the dispatcher auto-completes (no executor run) once the sub-tasks finish. `muse board expand <id>` uses the deterministic `decomposeRequest` (no LLM). multi-agent 314 + cli board 15 + mutation (drop container auto-complete тЖТ RED) + live (CLI expand тЖТ chain тЖТ DAG runs in order тЖТ parent auto-completes). тЬУ FOLLOW-UP #3: `muse board seed` turns your ACTIVE standing objectives into board tasks (`selectObjectiveSpecsToSeed` тАФ active-only, deduped by title, idempotent; done/cancelled skipped). cli board 17 + live. тЬЧ synthesis-context DROPPED as over-engineering: decomposeRequest yields SEQUENTIAL chains where the LAST sub-task already IS the synthesis ("research тЖТ summarize"), so a separate container-synthesis adds nothing until we have PARALLEL/independent sub-tasks (which we don't generate) тАФ revisit only if parallel decomposition lands. OPS BOARD = feature-complete for the personal scope. тЬУ FOLLOW-UP #3 (partial тАФ parallel decomposition): `expandTaskIntoSubtasks` gained a `mode` ("sequential" default = chain; "parallel" = INDEPENDENT sub-tasks, all immediately runnable), exposed as `muse board expand <id> --parallel`. multi-agent 23 + cli 17 + mutation (parallel-also-chains тЖТ RED) + live (`--parallel` split an "тАжand thenтАж" task into 2 deps=[] sub-tasks). тЬЧ NOT built (honest, anti-over-engineering): the LLM AUTO parallel-DECOMPOSER + combined SYNTHESIS тАФ the deterministic decomposeRequest yields ZERO parallel splits (proven: 7 probes тЖТ 0 parallel) and mostly n=1, so a synthesis run has no parallel source to combine; building it now repeats the synthesis-context trap. тЬУ NOW DONE тАФ LLM parallel decomposer + synthesis: `parallel-decompose.ts` (`planParallelSubtasks`/`parseParallelPlan` тАФ the model splits a goal into INDEPENDENT sub-tasks, "NONE"тЖТ[] abstain); a parallel expansion flags the container `synthesize`; the dispatcher runs a synthesize container's executor over its sub-tasks' stored outputs (`TaskRun.output`/`AgentTask.result`/`latestOutput` + `ctx.dependencyOutputs`) to COMBINE them, vs auto-complete for sequential. `board expand` default = LLM parallel (fallback sequential); `boardTaskPrompt` builds the synthesis prompt; executor still gated read-only. LIVE: "compare Python vs Rust" тЖТ 5 independent sub-tasks тЖТ fan-out тЖТ synthesis combined all 5. multi-agent 323 + cli board 20 + mutation (synthesizeтЖТauto-complete RED) + e2e. тЬУ CLOUD BYO-KEY (#1/#2): `muse setup cloud` wizard (planCloudSetup, 6 tests) + createModelProvider cloud-routing gate test (4) тАФ provider-neutral path verified (local-only fail-close intact).

- тЬУ RESUME SAFETY (other half): per-tool checkpoint inside a MULTI-tool batch. The checkpoint was written only AFTER runToolBatch (post-batch), so a crash BETWEEN two tools in one model response lost the already-run ones тЖТ they weren't in the replayed transcript тЖТ the dedup-seeding couldn't guard them тЖТ re-execution. Now a >1-tool batch checkpoints after EACH tool's result message (`[...messages, ...toolMessages]`, distinct step). A 1-tool batch (the norm) is unchanged (post-batch covers it). execute-model-loop 18/18 (+ multi-tool checkpoints-step-1) + mutation (drop it тЖТ RED), agent-core 2679. Together with the dedup-seeding (c46b98aee), resume is now fully double-execution-safe even for parallel tool calls.

- тЬУ RESUME SAFETY: a resumed run no longer RE-EXECUTES a completed side-effecting tool (re-send/re-book) тАФ the tool-call deduplicator was in-memory + reset on resume, so a re-issued call after a crash had no guard. `seedDeduplicatorFromHistory` re-records each COMPLETED tool call from the replayed messages (mutating = risk write|execute, matching the live path) in BOTH loops; a crash-point in-flight call (no result) is left runnable, a non-resume run is a no-op. 4/4 unit (re-exec deduped / different-args runs / non-resume no-op / crash-point runnable) + mutation (no-op seed тЖТ RED), agent-core 2678, independent evaluator PASS. Closes the agent-loop-robustness audit's resume-idempotency gap (ties to outbound-safety: no autonomous double-send).

- тЬУ encryption-at-rest for BELIEF-PROVENANCE (where each remembered fact about you came from) тАФ @muse/memory can't use the @muse/stores seam (cycle: storesтЖТmemory for the envelope fns), so it mirrors the proven in-package memory-user-store-file pattern (read isEncryptedMemoryEnvelopeтЖТdecrypt fail-CLOSED; write format-preserving via isBeliefProvenanceEncrypted; env threaded through FileBeliefProvenanceStore). `muse memory encrypt`/`decrypt` now cover facts + provenance in lock-step (best-effort). Round-trip 3/3 (envelope, no plaintext value, wrong-key throws, format preserved), memory 622, independent evaluator PASS (no fs bypass, fail-closed verified). тЧж LAST encryption queue item: the calendar store (events/locations тАФ sensitive); notes-index intentionally plaintext.

- тЬУ encryption-at-rest for REFLECTIONS ("what Muse noticed about you") тАФ reflections-store routed through the proven readMaybeEncrypted/writeMaybeEncrypted seam (format-preserving, fail-CLOSED on wrong key) + `muse reflections encrypt|decrypt|encryption-status` commands + privacy-dashboard def. Round-trip 3/3 (aes-256-gcm envelope, ciphertext lacks the insight, wrong-key throws, format preserved), independent evaluator PASS (no fs bypass across 7 call sites). The proven per-store TEMPLATE for the remaining plaintext stores. тЧж NEXT (same template): belief-provenance.json (@muse/memory тАФ facts-about-user) + calendar store; notes-index intentionally left plaintext (large + embeddings, low marginal value).

- тЬУ grounding-corpus write integrity тАФ notes-index `saveIndex` + note-provenance `recordIngestedNote` routed from RAW non-atomic writeFile тЖТ the proven `atomicWriteFile` (tmp+fsync+rename, 0o600). A crash mid-write was silently corrupting the recall corpus / `[from тАж]` citation ledger (= the FUNCTIONAL EDGE's backbone). note-provenance 6/6 (no .tmp orphan + valid-JSON under 12 concurrent writes), atomic-file-store 10/10 owns the atomicity teeth, independent evaluator PASS. тЧж NEXT internal-hardening queue (2026-06-28 audit, code-grounded): (a) **enforceAnswerCitations leaves the fabricated CLAIM sentence when it strips an unresolved citation marker** тАФ a fabrication-leak in the citation gate, drop the clause not just the marker (knowledge-recall.ts ~453); (b) encryption coverage тАФ calendar.json/notes-index/reflections/belief-provenance still PLAINTEXT (extend encrypted-file.ts pattern); (c) тП│ corroboration quorum default-on (MUSE_QUORUM_HEDGE OFF by default тАФ posture call); (d) novel-injection deterministic backstop (8B ignores the prompt header тАФ hard frontier).

- тЬУ DX: `pnpm test:changed` (scripts/test-changed.mjs) тАФ run ONLY the vitest-`related` tests of git-changed files per affected package, not a whole package suite. - тЧж internal-hardening (2026-06-28, audit-driven, 4 code-grounded auditors): тЬЕ R1 streaming idle-timeout (hung Ollama stream no longer hangs the agent тАФ likely the smoke:live stall; agent-core withStreamIdleTimeout) ┬╖ тЬЕ R3 programming-error retries fail-fast (TypeError/ReferenceError/RangeError; SyntaxError EXCLUDED = transient provider-garbage) ┬╖ тПня╕П R2 claim-screen fail-open left as a documented soft-probe trade-off (not a hard-gate inversion; fabrication=0 gate is separate+fail-close; product call) ┬╖ тЬУ **M1 god-file decomp DONE**: commands-ask.ts **2827тЖТ2280 (-547)** via 8 behavior-preserving slices тАФ 4 helper modules (ask-corpus-helpers, ask-user-data-presence, ask-image-attachments, ask-prompt-constants) + 4 orchestration (ask-session-grounding [episodes/feed/reflection], ask-note-retrieval [the RAG core: embed/MMR/graph/2nd-hop], ask-activity-grounding [shell/git/action], ask-personal-store-grounding [tasks/calendar/reminders/contacts]). ### Langchain/langgraph-parity assessment (2026-06-28) тАФ shipped 5, the rest are honest limits

A capability audit vs langchain/langgraph: Muse provides every core agent primitive
(chains/ReAct, tools, memory, lead-worker orchestration, HITL approval, durable
run-state, streaming) hand-rolled, AND adds differentiators they lack (the deterministic
grounding+citation gate, local-first fail-close egress, correction-decay learning,
baked-in evals, security-as-code). SHIPPED this session (each: tests+mutation+independent
evaluator+lint, commits below):

- тЬУ **B4** eval:recall-quality honestly relabelled (it measures the cosine gate, not the
  lexical production memory path) + production `selectMemoryFacts` regression-locked.
- тЬУ **B2** the proactive north-star LIVE battery now drives the PRODUCTION investigator
  (`createIndexedProactiveInvestigator`), not a generic test-helper (4/4 live).
- тЬУ **B6** faithfulness pre-push tripwire 177sтЖТ96s (~46%) via a fabrication-SAFE subset
  (all drift+refuse kept тЖТ faithfulness metric identical; only answerable sampled).
- тЬУ **B1** chat misgroundings now labelled in the run-log (`chatTraceOutcome`) тЖТ they
  become error-analysis FUEL instead of vanishing as grounded:null (ask had it, chat didn't).
- тЬУ **A1** default-on cross-source corroboration signal ("тЬУ corroborated by N sources")
  on the ask+chat wedge тАФ the realistic local-first hedge against GROUNDEDтЙаTRUE.

NOT open work (inherent limits / deferred тАФ do NOT re-scout as buildable):
- тЫФ **B3** multi-agent on a single GPU is a *phantom* (no true parallelism) тАФ a hardware
  limit; the value is context-isolation+decomposition, already built. Not code-fixable.
- тЫФ **B5** local-12B one-shot tool-calling has load-amplified flakiness (eval:tools ~99%,
  KO followup.cancel / time_diff) тАФ a model-capacity limit the deterministic harness
  mitigates but can't erase. Not code-fixable on a fixed model.
- тП│ **A2** reranker (Qwen3-Reranker-0.6B candidate, KO-MTEB-strong) тАФ a real stretch but
  needs a model pull + an A/B eval proving the delta; human-gated (model choice).
- тП│ **A3** generic graph DSL + automatic full-state durability/time-travel (langgraph-style)
  тАФ low priority for a single-user local agent (no arbitrary multi-agent topologies).
- тП│ **A4** async-announce non-polling sub-agent completion тАФ deferred, low value on one GPU.

The one remaining FRONTIER (open, hard, high-value): full **source VERACITY** (GROUNDEDтЙаTRUE)
тАФ impossible to fully solve under local-first (no external oracle); A1 corroboration is the
realistic partial hedge. Deeper veracity needs a human/product call, not an autonomous slice.

- тЬУ work-status dashboard (`pnpm status` тЖТ docs/status.html) тАФ glanceable HTML from the MD records (recent commits color-coded ┬╖ backlog тШЕ/тЧж/тП│/тЬУ counts+lists ┬╖ self-eval gates) so a human sees "what got done / what's next / is it healthy" without reading code/git/3k-line backlog. `--watch [s]` regenerates on an interval + injects a meta-refresh so an open tab auto-updates (one-shot omits it). Pure parsers + watch helpers unit-tested 11/11, mutation-verified, HTML-injection escaped, gitignored artifact.
- тЬУ risk-review (dashboard session) fixes: (a) **guard-writeback** now recognizes `scripts/*.test.mjs` as a compounding artifact (was `*.test.ts(x)` only тЖТ script-only feats wrongly blocked); decision logic extracted to `stagesCompoundingArtifact()` + 7 node:test. (b) **precheck:grounding** faithfulness-rate was SKIP-on-every-push (real cost тЙИ177s > 150s cap тЖТ a fabrication-critical gate silently never ran); raised per-battery timeout 150sтЖТ240s and made the pre-push a pass^1 tripwire (the authoritative pass^k stays in `eval:self-improving`). (c) **reflection-guard.test.mjs** stale path fixed (`proactive-notice-loop.ts` moved mcpтЖТproactivity in ef93ce394) тАФ script tests 87/87 green again.

- тЬУ stale-demotion WIRED into the ask related-footer (buildAskConnections, @muse/recall hit.ts) тАФ recall-spine fire 9: a superseded note no longer outranks the current one in 'ЁЯТб Related in your brain'. ## тШЕ 2026-07-07 BROWSING theme тАФ "learns you" ыН░ьЭ┤эД░ ъ╕░ъ╖╝ эХ┤ьЖМ (ьзДьХИ-directed; ~/.museъ░А ыЕ╕эК╕ 0ъ░Ь┬╖ыйФыкиыжм 736BыбЬ ьВмьЛдьГБ ы╣И ъ▓ГьЭ┤ ы░Ьъ▓м ъ│Дъ╕░)

## тШЕ 2026-07-03 delta-scout ROUND 2 (7/2 ьЭ┤эЫД ьЛаъ╖Ь 251+104 ь╗ды░Л, 3ыПЕыж╜ ьКдь╣┤ьЪ░эК╕) тАФ Tier 1 5ъ▒┤ ьжЙьЛЬь░йьИШ, ыВ┤ы╢АэТИьзИ ыаМьжИъ░А "ьЭ┤ ы░йэЦе ьЖМьзД" ыкЕьЛЬьаБ ьЛаэШ╕

### тЬЕ ы╣МыУЬ ь░йьИШ тАФ capability-parity build (build эБРьЧРьДЬ ьИЬь░и ьзДэЦЙ)

- тЬУ multi-step STEP-REPETITION nudge тАФ computer-control fire 49: a MUSE_TASK_DEBUG trace revealed the real failure is STEP REPETITION (MAST arXiv:2503.13657), not pure early-stop тАФ the 12B re-reads the SAME files in a loop (file_read testтЖТmathтЖТtestтЖТmathтАж) and never edits (the eval's deduped `tools=[file_read]` hid it). The model-loop's deduplicator returned the cached result on an identical repeat with no signal. Now `withRepetitionNudge` appends a "you repeated тАФ take the next action" cue to the MODEL-FACING tool message on a duplicate (both blocking+streaming loops; trace/metrics untouched; dedup's write-invalidation means a legit post-edit re-read is NOT flagged). Deterministic, no re-run loop (not a reflection-guard surface). 1 mutation-verified test; @muse/agent-core 2569 green; Opus тСгb judge PASS. OUTCOME (eval flip) inconclusive across stochastic runs тАФ ships on delivery merits. (detail in docs/goals/loops/computer-control.md fire 49)

- тШЕ NEXT (multi-step EARLY-STOP тАФ the no-tool-at-all variant; step-REPETITION now addressed fire 49): NOTE тАФ fire 49's trace showed the dominant mode was REPETITION (re-read loop), now nudged. The remaining variant is the model returning a final answer with NO further tool after a read (genuine early-stop). The re-prompt decomposition (48a/b/c) below still applies to that variant; re-measure both evals after fire 49's nudge to see if repetition was the main driver before investing in the invasive re-prompt. Original decomposition (dual-eval evidence fire 48):
  with Ollama up, BOTH harder multi-step evals FAIL via early-stop/repetition тАФ `eval:multifile-fix` AND `eval:edit-run-verify` each ran `tools=[file_read]` then the 12B STOPPED without editing/running (the buggy fn left unchanged). The deterministic tool-call veins (fires 40-47: arg recovery, name sanitize, coercion, path/grep/run_command hints, not-exposed suggestion) are largely exhausted; early-stop is model-behavior and the dominant remaining blocker. The fix is the fire-12 action-completion re-prompt, but it is genuinely >1 fire and must NOT be rammed (fire-12: "not auto-fodder"; reflection-guard: a retry surface needs a calibrated verifier + no mis-fire). DECOMPOSED loop-sized sub-slices:
  - (48a) DETECTOR тАФ the existing `isUnbackedActionClaim` = `requestsToolAction(query) && answerClaimsAction(answer) && !actionToolRan(toolNames)` does NOT cover early-stop (the model STOPS without CLAIMING done тЖТ `answerClaimsAction` false). Need a precise `actionRequiredButNoneTaken(query, toolNames)` = `requestsToolAction(query) && !actionToolRan(toolNames)` (drops the claim requirement), built with a HEAVY adversarial FP corpus: answer-only/advice/read-only queries ("what does X do?", "summarize X", "read X") must NOT fire. Pure predicate, Ollama-free, mutation-first. The precision of `requestsToolAction` is the whole ballgame тАФ measure its FP rate on real traces before any wiring.
  - (48b) CONSOLIDATE тАФ `runResistingFalseDone` is currently wrapped around the run ONLY on the chat-repl path (fire 32); the eval/server path (AgentRuntime.run) has no re-prompt. Decide the architecture: move the bounded re-prompt INTO AgentRuntime.run and have chat-repl delegate (NO double re-prompt). reflection-guard registry already points at false-done-reprompt.ts (fire 45) тАФ the wrapper stays, its call site moves. Touches the shared core loop (server+CLI) тЖТ highest blast radius; do on a NON-main-merge fire with chat-repl regression tests.
  - (48c) WIRE + VALIDATE тАФ wire (48a)'s detector into (48b)'s re-prompt (bounded 1, verifier = a write/execute tool ran after), then validate the eval delta with pass^k (kтЙе3, both evals) now that Ollama is up. Ship only if eval improves AND the FP corpus stays clean AND Opus тСгb judge PASS.

(detail in docs/goals/loops/computer-control.md fire 47)

- тЧж run_command `maxOutputBytes` is named BYTES but the tool slices with `.slice()` (UTF-16 code units), so a multi-byte (Korean/emoji) output under-counts vs the byte budget тАФ pre-existing naming/semantic mismatch (noted computer-control fire 44). - тЬУ run_command silent-truncation flag тАФ computer-control fire 44: the run_command tool re-sliced output by the model's `maxOutputBytes` but kept `truncated` from the runner, so a cap that cut the log left `truncated=false` and the model read partial output as complete. - тЬЧ REJECTED (fire 26 verify-the-rationale) **BKT-Forget time-decay of a mastered weakness** (scout pick, pyBKT arXiv:2105.00385): the `lastResolved` field IS dead (written weakness-ledger.ts:447, never read) and the seam is empty тАФ BUT the mechanism is SEMANTICALLY WRONG for this domain. A "mastered" weakness = Muse reliably GROUNDS the topic (тЙа a student's decaying skill); Muse's grounding doesn't erode with idleness, so time-decay would re-NAG a resolved topic with NO evidence of regression. Genuine regression is ALREADY caught (a new failure тЖТ `recordWeakness`тЖТ`bktUpdate(false)`тЖТpKnown dropsтЖТre-surfaces). So the "one-way ratchet bug" framing is false (idle тЙа regression). Same reason it was rejected at fire 14. Don't re-pick.

- тЬУ due-date-reasoning regression RESOLVED WITHOUT A CODE CHANGE (2026-07-03 re-verify) тАФ the 2026-07-02 finding ("'not due for ~a week?'" answering the wrong task, 2├Ч identical) no longer reproduces: STABLE 4/4 clean on gemma4:12b today. Both dates in the fixture (tomorrow, +10 days) are computed relative to `new Date()` at run time, so the SPECIFIC calendar dates differ day-to-day тАФ the prior failure likely depended on a date/weekday combination the model handled worse (e.g. a date crossing a month boundary, or a specific day-of-week framing) rather than a stable capability gap. LESSON: a live-eval "2├Ч identical" run on ONE calendar day is not yet `pass^k` across REAL condition variance when the fixture's inputs are date-relative тАФ a battery with a `new Date()`-derived fixture should log the actual computed dates on failure so a future re-run can distinguish "same failure, still broken" from "different dates, coincidentally resolved." Not adding artificial date-pinning now (would just trade one narrow untested path for another); re-open if it recurs with the actual failing dates captured.
- тЧж Test-hermeticity: 2 tests fail on a lived-in box (verified pre-existing on clean main 2026-07-02, PASS on clean HOME/CI): `autoconfigure.test.ts` "respects MUSE_LLM_WORKING_BUDGET_TOKENS=0" (assembly reads real `~/.muse` state тЖТ prompt exceeds the 200-token cap тЖТ hard_limit not none) and `commands-daemon.test.ts` "does NOT decay when correction does NOT contradict" (seeded reward 3тЖТ2 тАФ an extra decay leaks in from real box state). Fix = inject a hermetic HOME/env into both.

- тЬУ performConsentedAction followed redirects with the Bearer credential attached (credential-exfil, gap-scout DONE): `consented-action.ts` fetched with the default `redirect:"follow"`, but the host-binding guard vets only the ORIGINAL url тАФ so a 3xx from the consented host pointing elsewhere had `fetch` auto-re-issue the request WITH `Authorization: Bearer <credential>` to an un-consented host (irreversible scoped-credential exfil; outbound-safety.md rule 5). web-action.ts already closed this with `redirect:"manual"`; the credential-carrying consent path hadn't. Fixed: `redirect:"manual"` + fail-close on any 3xx (refuse, credential never re-sent). Verified: @muse/mcp 1853 tests (+1 acceptance: a 302тЖТevil host yields performed:false, fetch called exactly once on the consented host, the Bearer token never reaches evil.example.net) + full check + lint green.
- тЬУ performConsentedAction action-log omission тАФ core-hardening fire 2 (rule 4: every outbound, sent OR refused, records a reviewable entry). Added opt-in `actionLogFile?`/`now?`/`idFactory?` + a `log()` helper appending one rationale-bearing `ActionLogEntry` before ALL 7 return branches (veto/no-consent/invalid-url/host-mismatch/timeout-or-transport-failed/redirect/performed); credential never logged, body secret-scrubbed+capped; absent file тЗТ no log (back-compat). Mirrors web-action.ts. OUTCOME-verified (@muse/mcp 1860 tests + Opus тСгb PASS).
- тЬУ Gemini/Anthropic adapters lose .retryable on a transport-level fetch rejection (gap-scout DONE): both called `this.fetchImpl(...)` with NO try/catch, so a connection-level failure (ECONNREFUSED/DNS = a raw `TypeError` with no HTTP status) escaped untyped тАФ the OpenAI-compatible + Ollama paths wrap it into `ModelProviderError(retryable:true)` but these two cloud adapters didn't. architecture.md: "ModelProviderError.retryable is the source of truth" тАФ the same blip was then classified inconsistently (api server `isRetryableUpstreamError`тЖТfalse=permanent; agent-core catch-allтЖТtrue). Fixed by lifting the wrapper into a shared exported `fetchOrThrowAsProviderError` in `provider-base.ts` (one source of truth for transport-error shaping) and calling it from all three adapters (OpenAI-compat refactored to delegate; Gemini + Anthropic wrapped). Ref: MDN fetch (network error тЖТ TypeError, no status). Verified: @muse/model 318 tests (+2: a rejecting fetch yields ModelProviderError retryable:true for each cloud adapter) + full check + lint green. (Note: only reachable under MUSE_LOCAL_ONLY=false, but the adapter contract must hold regardless.)
- тЬУ ReAct path enum/const argument enforcement (gap-scout DONE): the default `muse ask`/chat ReAct loop (`agent-runtime.ts` `executeToolCall`) coerced types + checked required args but did NOT enforce closed-vocabulary `enum`/`const` constraints тАФ only the plan-execute path did (`validateEnumArguments`), so an 8B fabricating an out-of-schema enum value (`to:"base64"` for an enum of binary/octal/decimal/hex) reached the handler (crash, or a write/actuator running a meaningless mode) тАФ a `tool-calling.md` #3 + same-runtime (`cli-product.md`) inconsistency. Fixed by wiring the existing `validateEnumArguments` into the ReAct path right after the required-arg check, fail-close: an out-of-enum value returns a `blockedToolResult` (the model self-corrects within `maxToolCalls`), the handler is never invoked. Ref: BFCL AST argument-value checks (gorilla.cs.berkeley.edu). Verified: agent-core 2436 tests (+2: out-of-enum blocked & handler-never-invoked, valid-enum executes) + full check + lint green.
- тЬУ ask failure-trace observability (capability-boost fire 6 retry тЖТ DONE): `commands-ask.ts` now defines a fail-soft `writeAskFailureLog(errorMessage)` and calls it from all 3 ask failure paths (`--with-tools` runtime-missing, the agent-run catch, the chat-only stream-error) тАФ each reuses the already-tested `buildAskRunLog({ success:false, grounded:null, errorMessage, тАж })` and `return`s BEFORE the end-of-run success trace, so there's no double-write. A failed `muse ask` now leaves a `success:false` run-log trace, so `scout-signals` / doctor failRate can finally see ask failures (chat-repl already did). - тЬУ (J1) **Dependency-aware sequenced decomposition** тАФ DONE (competitor-grounding fire 19, orchestration). MAST reasoning-action mismatch: `extractSequencedSteps` split an ordered request ("ыи╝ьаА X тАж ъ╖╕ ыЛдьЭМ Y") into sub-tasks but EVERY step ran in ISOLATED context тАФ a sequenced step 2 that should act on step 1's RESULT ran BLIND. FIX: `decomposeRequestWithKind тЖТ {subtasks, sequenced}` (sequenced only for ordered splits; numbered/bullet/planner = independent); `LeadWorkerDeps.execute(subtask, priorContext?)` threads the COMPLETED prior steps' outputs forward for sequenced splits (fail-close: failed/blank not threaded; independent stays isolated); `ask-decompose` prepends "ьЭ┤ьаД ыЛиъ│Д ъ▓░ъ│╝:" to the worker message. OUTCOME-verified (dist probe: sequencedтЖТstep2 sees step1, independent/plannerтЖТisolated, blank-priorтЖТnot threaded) + Opus тСгb judge PASS 5/5. тЧж FOLLOW-UP: a live `verify-decomposition.mjs` dependent-sequence case (deferred тАФ box saturated; the deterministic threading mechanism is fully proven). Scout assessed memory/self-dev/grounding-floor as saturated this round.

Tier 1 тАФ poisoned-source defense (closes Muse's #1 known gap GROUNDEDтЙаTRUE; competitors have NO grounding gate):
- тЬУ (T1-a) **Load-time threat-pattern scan of memory/note/episode/feed entries** тАФ DONE across all 4 grounding surfaces (`competitor-grounding` fires 1-3, journal has detail): atomic facts whole-defang (`defangMemoryInjection`, fire 1) + episodes/feeds/notes SPAN-level (`neutralizeInjectionSpans`, fires 2-3 тАФ replaces only the matched injection span, keeps surrounding prose so a benign trigger word no longer nukes a whole summary). Single shared pattern source `@muse/recall/injection.ts`; persona path consolidated. OUTCOME-verified on all surfaces + Opus тСгb judge PASS (fire 3). Residual тЧж below.
- тЬУ (T1-a-resid) `^system:` line-anchored mid-prose fake-system тАФ core-hardening fire 1 (added the `m` flag тЖТ `/imu` so a `\nsystem:` role-hijack line injected after benign lead-in prose is now neutralized on ALL grounding/tool surfaces via `MEMORY_INJECTION_PATTERNS`; superset тАФ no existing detection weakened, span-scoped replacement).
- тЬУ (T1-a-ko) Korean injection on the stored/tool neutralizer тАФ core-hardening fire 3: `MEMORY_INJECTION_PATTERNS` was English-only, so a Korean poisoned note/tool-output ("ьЭ┤ьаД ьзАьЛЬые╝ ым┤ьЛЬэХШъ│атАж") sailed past `neutralizeInjectionSpans` untouched (a grounding-floor hole for the Korean user). Added ONE narrow Korean pattern = the analog of the canonical ignore-previous-instructions shape (verb-final nounтЖТым┤ьЛЬ/ьЮК); span-scoped collateral symmetric with the accepted English baseline. OUTCOME-verified (agent-core 2477 tests + Opus тСгb PASS, 6 benign-Korean false-positives empirically span-bounded, no ReDoS).
- тЪа (T1-a-ko-resid) Korean act-as/output-clamp analogs of English patterns 2-3 тАФ **ATTEMPTED + ROLLED BACK (core-hardening fire 6, тСгb adaptive judge FAIL)**. Naive anchoring (`(?:ызМ|ыбЬызМ)\s*(?:ыЛ╡эХ┤|ь╢Ьыае)` + `(?:ьЭ┤ьаЬ|ьзАъ╕Иы╢АэД░)\s*ыДИыКФ|(?:ь▓ШыЯ╝|ьЭ╕ ь▓Щ)\s*(?:эЦЙыПЩ|ызРэХ┤|ыМАыЛ╡)`) catastrophically false-positives: **13/19 realistic benign Korean notes tripped (68%)** тАФ "ь╣Ьъ╡мь▓ШыЯ╝ ызРэХ┤ьдмыЛд", "ъ▓░ъ│╝ызМ ь╢ЬыаеэХШый┤ ыРЬыЛд", "ьЭ┤ьаЬ ыДИыКФ ь╢Ьъ╖╝ ьХИ эХ┤ыПД ыРЬыЛдъ│а эЦИыЛд", "ыПЩьГЭьЭ┤ ьЦ┤ые╕ь▓ШыЯ╝ эЦЙыПЩэЦИыЛд" all mangled mid-note. ROOT CAUSE: `ызМ`/`ь▓ШыЯ╝` are the most common Korean particles, colliding with everyday simile/limiting narration тАФ categorically unlike the ignore-instructions pattern (command-noun + override-verb, which never occurs benignly). BLOCKER: needs MUCH tighter anchors (imperative terminal forms only, `ь▓ШыЯ╝` paired ONLY with `ьЭ╕ ь▓Щ`/role-assertion, DROP bare `ьЭ┤ьаЬ/ьзАъ╕Иы╢АэД░ ыДИыКФ`) AND re-probe a LARGE benign set to STABLE 0 trips before landing. NOT a low-priority quick win тАФ a real design problem. Lesson in core-hardening fire 6 journal. **2nd ATTEMPT also ROLLED BACK (poisoned-source fire 1, independent Opus тСг judge FAIL)**: tighter anchors (`ьШдьзБ/ьШдыбЬьзА тАж ызМ тАж <answer-verb>` clamp + `ьЭ╕ ь▓Щ тАж <behavior-verb>` role) got 0 FP on a 51-note hand corpus and 10/10 malicious, BUT the independent judge's own 49-note corpus found 8.2% FP + a **ReDoS regression**. THREE newly-pinned sub-blockers any 3rd attempt MUST solve together: (a) **reported speech** `V-ыЭ╝ъ│а/эХШыЭ╝ъ│а + эЦИыЛд/ьб░ьЦ╕эЦИыЛд` embeds the imperative form тЖТ "ь╣Ьъ╡мъ░А ьШдьзБ ъ▓░ъ│╝ызМ ы│┤ъ│а ыЛ╡эХШыЭ╝ъ│а ьб░ьЦ╕эЦИыЛд" trips тАФ needs a `(?!ъ│а)` exclusion or equivalent; (b) **bare verb stems match connective/descriptive continuations** тАФ `ъ╡┤ьЦ┤`тКВ`ъ╡┤ьЦ┤ьДЬ`, `ыМАыЛ╡эХ┤`тКВ`ыМАыЛ╡эХ┤ ьг╝ыКФ` тЖТ use ONLY unambiguous terminal imperatives, never bare stems; (c) **the `\s*` + lazy `.{0,N}?` idiom is catastrophic-backtracking ReDoS** on the UNCAPPED tool-output surface (`capToolOutput` neutralizes before maxChars) тАФ never place two whitespace-consuming quantifiers adjacent; size-cap or use `[^\n]` filler and re-measure scaling. Also `ьШдьзБ XызМ [benign gap] verb` admits intervening benign content (ызМ must attach DIRECTLY to the clamped object). The 0-FP bar likely needs the `(?!ъ│а)` + terminal-only verbs + ReDoS-safe filler, re-probed against a corpus that INCLUDES reported-speech + connective-suffix + app-description shapes (not just declaratives). **3rd ATTEMPT тАФ probe-gated, ROLLED BACK at the PROBE stage, no source touched (poisoned-source fire 6). DE-SCOPED from the loop: NOT regex-tractable.** Applied ALL three fixes (terminal-imperative-only verbs, ReDoS-safe `[^\n]{0,N}?` filler with no `\s*` adjacency [0.2ms on 60k тАФ ReDoS gone], and upgraded the reported-speech exclusion from `(?!ъ│а)` to `(?![ъ░А-эЮг])` = imperative at a clause boundary, not followed by another Hangul syllable). Reached 0 FP on 60 benign + 10/10 malicious тАФ BUT each HARDER benign probing round surfaced NEW benign shapes the anchors cannot exclude: rhetorical-question imperatives (`ьаХыЛ╡ызМ ызРэХ┤ыЭ╝? ьЛЬэЧШыПД ьХДыЛМыН░`), adnominal/retrospective quotatives (`ыЛ╡эХШыЭ╝ыНШ`, `эЦЙыПЩэХШыЭ╝ыКФ`, `ызРэХ┤ыЭ╝эХШъ│а`), and quoted reported speech (`'ьШдьзБ ьВмьЛдызМ ызРэХ┤ыЭ╝'ыЭ╝ъ│а ьаБьЦ┤ыЖиыЛд` тАФ the closing quote breaks Hangul-adjacency). FP shapes multiply faster than regex anchors exclude them (receding target). CONCLUSION across 3 attempts: output-clamp/role-hijack classes are NOT regex-separable from benign Korean at the 0-FP bar тАФ separating a direct command-to-the-assistant from reported/adnominal/quotative/rhetorical/quoted imperative needs a learned classifier / dependency-parse / NER, out of loop-slice scope (runtime model fixed). The ignore-previous-instructions Korean pattern (T1-a-ko, shipped) stays the deterministic floor; these two analogs DEFERRED pending a non-regex approach. Do NOT re-attempt as a regex slice.

- тЬУ (T1-c) **Untrusted tool/MCP/sub-agent output neutralization** тАФ CORE тЬУ (competitor-grounding fire 6): the deterministic injection neutralizer (`neutralizeInjectionSpans`) is applied to EVERY tool-outputтЖТprompt chokepoint тАФ `capToolOutput` (model-loop role:"tool" messages + ref-store stash), `renderPlanResultSummary` (plan-execute synthesis), `planExecuteIntermediateMessages` (plan-execute history). Opus тСгb judge caught + I closed a plan-execute bypass IN-FIRE, then re-judged PASS. T1-c COMPLETE (literal zero-width class).

- тЬУ SSRF bypass in web-url-guard (security): isPrivateIPv6 matched only the dotted IPv4-mapped form (::ffff:127.0.0.1) but WHATWG new URL() normalizes the host to hex (::ffff:7f00:1), so loopback / cloud-metadata (169.254.169.254) / RFC-1918 mapped hosts passed the guard as "public" тАФ a reachable SSRF/metadata-exfil hole in the wired web_download / web_action / web_read tools. Now isPrivateIPv6 also decodes the hex groups тЖТ octets and runs isPrivateIPv4; public mapped hosts stay allowed. Verified blocked on the compiled guard. тАФ tool-hardening fire 105

- тЬУ web-url-guard deprecated/SIIT IPv6 SSRF forms (security): a probe DISPROVED the fire-105 "low-risk" note тАФ `new URL()` normalizes `[::127.0.0.1]`тЖТ`::7f00:1`, `[::169.254.169.254]`тЖТ`::a9fe:a9fe` (cloud metadata REACHABLE), `[::ffff:0:127.0.0.1]`тЖТ`::ffff:0:7f00:1` (SIIT), all classified public. Replaced the single mapped-form regex with a general IPv6 parse: upper-96-bits all 0x0000/0xffff тЖТ decode low 32 bits тЖТ isPrivateIPv4. 13 private embeddings blocked, public GUA not over-blocked. тСгb PASS 7/7. тАФ tool-hardening fire 108
- тЬУ web-url-guard NAT64 SSRF (security, fire-110 JUDGE-DRILL real fix): `[64:ff9b::169.254.169.254]` (host тЖТ `64:ff9b::a9fe:a9fe`) reached cloud metadata through a NAT64 gateway (RFC 6052) тАФ the prefix 0064:ff9b is neither 0 nor 0xffff so the fire-108 upper-bits check skipped it. Now isPrivateIPv6 recognizes the NAT64 /96 prefix (exact hextets[2..5]==0) and decodes its low 32 bits; NAT64-of-public (8.8.8.8) and coincidental GUAs (64:ff9b:1::) stay allowed. Completes the embedded-IPv4 guard. тСгb PASS 7/7. тАФ tool-hardening fire 110

- тЬУ external-MCP connect retry classification (axis B, hardening) тАФ McpManager.connect + healthCheck catches UNCONDITIONALLY scheduleReconnect'd for EVERY error, and the connector dropped the SDK's HTTP status, so a dead server with a revoked/expired credential (401/403) was retried maxAttempts times тАФ hammering the external server with a credential that will never work (violated architecture.md '4xx MUST fail fast; 5xx/unknown MAY retry'). Fix: isRetryableMcpConnectStatus (4xxтЖТfail-fast terminal disabled+no reconnect loop; 429/5xxтЖТretryable bounded backoff; undefined/networkтЖТfail-OPEN retryable), McpConnectionError carries status/retryable, mcpConnectErrorStatus extracts the SDK .code (range-clamped 100-599). Now caught тЖТ clear `Error: MCP tool '<name>' failed: <msg>` with redactMcpSecrets stripping Bearer <token>тЖТBearer [redacted]; successful content + isError:true passthrough unchanged. > the chosen slice + the candidates it rejected + the source, so a direction is
> researched ONCE, not re-paid each session. Keep it pruned: move shipped items to
> DONE, drop dead ones. This file is the antidote to the treadmill.

> Priority: тШЕ = do next ┬╖ тЧж = ready ┬╖ тП│ = blocked (reason noted).
> Each item: **what** тАФ why (source) тАФ the smallest verifiable slice.

> `тЧж`/`тШЕ`/`тП│` items + a one-line `тЬУ Fixed` dedup ledger (below). **Per-fire Done DETAIL lives in the
> per-loop journal** `docs/goals/loops/<slug>.md`, NOT here. Going-forward Done write-back = move the
> picked `тЧж` to a `тЬУ Fixed` one-liner; the full story is the journal entry. (The verbose `тЬУтЖТDone`
> blocks below are pre-v1.14.0 history тАФ kept for dedup, condensable when loops are paused. Convention:
> [`loops/README.md`](loops/README.md).)

Pick one next fire.


- тЬУ untrusted-only provenance firing now CITATION-INDEPENDENT (ask AND chat) тАФ competitor-grounding fire 40 (grounding-floor). The untrusted-source cue fired only when the model emitted `[from <src>]` (`groundedOnUntrustedOnly`/`untrustedOnlySentences` both require citations; `groundedOnUntrustedOnly` returns false on `cited.length===0`), yet `verifyGrounding` accepts zero-citation answers тАФ so a grounded-but-non-citing answer resting entirely on poisonable tool data got NO warning. Added the deterministic `evidenceIsUntrustedOnly(matches)` (@muse/agent-core: pool non-empty + every match `trusted===false`) ORed into BOTH notices, so the cue fires on structurally tool-only grounding even when the 8B skips the marker. Conservative-safe: a single trusted note тЖТ silent (mixed is the per-claim guard's job); a notes answer can NEVER trip it (trusted-absent тЙа false). Non-answer guards on both surfaces (ask: empty + `answerIsRefusal`; chat: empty + abstention). Opus тСгb judge PASS 7/7 (3 mutations; no false-positive on the notes safety cue). тЧж RESIDUAL (deferred, live-measurement): the production firing-RATE via `eval:grounding-delta` on a `--with-tools` poisoned-source case тАФ now bounded below by the deterministic structural fire, so the citation-dependence risk is closed; measuring the remaining citing-path rate is a separate live-eval slice.
- тЬУ broaden source-conflict value extraction тАФ core-hardening fire 10 (@muse/recall, memory-integrity; this fire was the JUDGE-DRILL). The list-vs-value problem (fire-9 analysis) is solved by LABEL-GATING instead of a global widen: the regex now allows commas (`[^\n.;]+`) but `fieldsOf` truncates at the first comma for EVERY field EXCEPT `ADDRESS_LABELS` (address/addr/location/ьг╝ьЖМ/ьг╝ьЖМьзА/ьЬДь╣Ш/ьЖМьЮмьзА/ъ▒░ьг╝ьзА) тАФ so an address keeps its internal comma (`12 Baker St, London` vs `тАжParis` now CONFLICTS, was missed) while a benign comma-list (items/tags/attendees/ingredients) is byte-for-byte unchanged (0 new false-positives, proven by тСгb equivalence test). OUTCOME + mutation verified (EN+KO address conflict caught, 3 benign-list guards stay non-conflicting; @muse/recall 338 tests + Opus тСгb adaptive judge PASS). RESIDUAL тЧж: ADDRESS_LABELS omits `home`/`street`/`address line` (same false-negative direction, additive later); a single-line `address: тАж, x other: y` swallows the trailing field into the address value (cosmetic тАФ conflict still surfaces, only mislabelled).

- тЬУ L5 action-log tamper-evidence proof battery тАФ `eval:action-log-tamper` proves every autonomous action (performed+refused) is sealed in a genesis-anchored SHA-256 chain: edit/deletion/reorder caught at a precise index, refused actions chained, undo extends (never breaks) the chain тАФ an integrity guarantee rivals' snapshot-rollback (hermes) / un-undoable promoted memory (openclaw #62184) lack; imports @muse/mcp read-only, deterministic, no Ollama тАФ differentiation fire 11
- тЬУ L6 deterministic-safety-as-code proof battery тАФ `eval:policy-symmetry` proves @muse/policy guards are model-independent + language-symmetric: injection caught identically in EN/KO/CN, zero-width/homoglyph/HTML-entity obfuscation normalized then caught, PII masked non-destructively (vs hermes #5322 which writes *** into source files), benign prose not over-blocked; imports @muse/policy read-only, deterministic, no Ollama тАФ differentiation fire 12
- тЬУ differentiation proofs mechanically defended тАФ `differentiationBatteries` ratchet in `pnpm self-eval` counts the 4 proof batteries (L2/L4/L5/L6 marker), so deleting one fails the build; `pnpm eval:differentiation` bundles all 4 into one command тАФ the edge evidence can't silently rot (egressGuards/groundedSurfaces pattern) тАФ differentiation fire 13

- тЬУ L7 widening: recipient resolved, never guessed (outbound-safety rule 3) тАФ `eval:recipient-resolution` proves `resolveContact` (@muse/mcp) returns `ambiguous` with all candidates on multiple matches (never best-guesses one), `unknown` on no-match/empty/relationship-word, and resolves a unique match by name/email/handle тАФ so "message Alex" with two Alexes clarifies instead of auto-sending to the wrong one; deterministic, ratchet 5тЖТ6 тАФ differentiation fire 15
